======== Scenario: col_kitchen ========
Session Sequence: Butcher
----- Session: Butcher -----
Synopsis: This dialog is started by talking to the Butcher character in the Colony. The player may ask the Butcher questions or recruit them as a temporary follower inside the Colony. Alternatively, this dialog runs through a flag in case the player has already met the Butcher, or if the Butcher was recruited as a follower. The Butcher sounds eerily vacant unless otherwise specified, his mind destroyed by his time in Colony.

Chop: ... || [context] NodeContext: Silent

======== Scenario: col_elderbrain ========
Session Sequence: AD_Rapid01 -> AD_Rapid02
----- Session: AD_Rapid01 -----
Synopsis: Quick-fire Elder Brain ADs in the Colony corridors. If the party attacked Ketheric on the Moonrise Rooftop, there will be more frantic, fast-paced ADs from the Elder Brain surrounding us in quick succession, similar to when we approach the Elder Brain in the Morphic Pool. In this flow, the evacuation of the Colony is a lot more pressing because Ketheric was attacked.

: ---DESCEND--- || [context] NodeContext: frantic

----- Session: AD_Rapid02 -----
Synopsis: Quick-fire Elder Brain ADs in the Colony corridors. If the party attacked Ketheric on the Moonrise Rooftop, there will be more frantic, fast-paced ADs from the Elder Brain surrounding us in quick succession, similar to when we approach the Elder Brain in the Morphic Pool. In this flow, the evacuation of the Colony is a lot more pressing because Ketheric was attacked.

: ---ASSEMBLE--- || [context] NodeContext: Frantic

======== Scenario: col_kitchenentry ========
Session Sequence: PAD
----- Session: PAD -----
Synopsis: The party comments on the gruesome smell and/or appearance of the Colony's kitchen and dissection room.

Player: The stench. I wonder how many pilgrimages to Moonrise ended down here. || [context] NodeContext: Entering a room that smells disgusting

======== Scenario: col_general ========
Session Sequence: PAD_CallLiftFail -> PAD_ElevatorBanter
----- Session: PAD_CallLiftFail -----
Synopsis: The player has tried to call the platform in COL while it's already at the level in question.

Player: The platform's already here.

----- Session: PAD_ElevatorBanter -----
Synopsis: A banter PAD when taking the elevator down to the Ketheric Showdown from the upper floor of the Colony. If there are two tadpoled players available, they will banter together, otherwise a solo PAD will play.

Player: Is anyone else's tadpole squirming around a lot more than usual?
Player: Aye. Feels like something down here has them excited... or scared.

======== Scenario: col_necrolab ========
Session Sequence: GrandDesignSculpture
----- Session: GrandDesignSculpture -----
Synopsis: An interaction with the mind flayer sculpture depicting the Grand Design, as seen in the intro cutscene of the game in the Nautiloid. A psionic imprint tells you its story.

Narrator: -OUR-<br>                     -destiny-<br>-DESIGN-<br>                 -downfall- || [context] CinematicNodeContext: Wide shot of entire relief, dwarfing player

======== Scenario: sce_partyvb ========
Session Sequence: PAD_ToBaldursGate -> PAD_ShadowCurseNotLifted -> PAD_UnfinishedBusiness
----- Session: PAD_ToBaldursGate -----
Synopsis: After leaving Ketheric's throne room after Ketheric's defeat, a player character comments on what they need to do next - head for Baldur's Gate.

Player: The road to Baldur's Gate is west of the town. If we hurry, we'll arrive before the Absolute's forces.

----- Session: PAD_ShadowCurseNotLifted -----
Synopsis: If the shadow curse wasn't lifted, the party will remark that we still need protection against the curse despite Ketheric having been defeated.

Player: Ketheric may be gone, but the shadows remain. On our guard. || [context] NodeContext: SH: 'the shadow curse remains' = SH has abandoned Shar. 'Lady Shar's power persists' = SH loyal to shar.

----- Session: PAD_UnfinishedBusiness -----
Synopsis: After the act 2 epilogue, the party comments on resolving unfinished business before moving on to Baldur's Gate/act 3.

Player: The road to Baldur's Gate is up ahead. No turning back, once we start down that road.

======== Scenario: sce_isobelnightsongreunion ========
Session Sequence: 
----- Session:  -----
Synopsis: If Isobel and Nightsong survive Act 2 they will be having a heartfelt reunion during the Epilogue

Isobel: Ah! There you are. This is Aylin. Aylin, this is -
Nightsong: We have met. The instigator of my despair - and then my elation.
Nightsong: We must watch this one closely, Isobel. Their motivations are suspect - aye, suspect indeed.
Isobel: Hmm - it sounds like we have much to discuss. Perhaps we could join you in your camp later?
Isobel: I have more to thank you for than I knew. And we have much to discuss. Perhaps we could join you in your camp later?
Player: Firstly, allow me to apologise to Dame Aylin. My actions were strategy - not personal. || [approval] ['Karlach 1', 'Gale 1', 'Wyll 1', 'Astarion 1', 'Shadowheart 1', "Lae'zel 1", 'Minthara 1']
Nightsong: My forgiveness will be the same. I'd be a fool to turn down a powerful ally - especially one who has earned the trust of fair Isobel.
Nightsong: But Dame Aylin's life is neverending. And she does not forget. Now - I believe Isobel asked a question of you. We will meet you in your camp - is it agreed?
Player: It's a little crowded already.
Isobel: We'll make our visit brief. Cleric's honour.
Player: I doubt that. You go your way, and I'll go mine.
Nightsong: We are not welcome, my love. No matter. We will hie us to the Hill of the Headless Dancer and bare our flesh beneath the cleansing light of the moon's soft gaze.
Isobel: A hundred years hasn't changed you at all, my love. As for you - if we aren't to meet again, I'll say my thank-yous. And my goodbyes. || [context] NodeContext: First part to Aylin, Second part to player
Isobel: If we meet again, it will be my pleasure.

======== Scenario: sce_halsin ========
Session Sequence: 
----- Session:  -----
Synopsis: Dialogue with Halsin in the epilogue of Act 2. In it, he reacts to the various states that could occur in relation to his desire to rid the Act 2 region of the shadow curse:- if you've already done everything needed to ensure success. he's grateful and seeks to remain with you on the journey to Baldur's Gate.- if the curse is not yet sure to be lifted, but there's still something that can be done (ie Thaniel was saved from the Shadowfell, but hasn't been fully restored), he will implore the players to help and offer to join them.- if it's no longer possible to lift the curse, Halsin is sad and resigned to staying behind to stand sentry over it. He will not be available as a companion in Act 3, and his story effectively ends here.

Halsin: Thaniel rests still, but it's no easy slumber. || [context] NodeContext: Concerned/Urgent. The curse will not be lifted unless a spirit of the land is fully restored
Halsin: The shadows rended him in two when they bore him away to the Shadowfell. Half of his essence remained here, amidst the curse. || [context] NodeContext: Concerned/Urgent. The curse will not be lifted unless a spirit of the land is fully restored
Halsin: What stayed behind would have been the strongest part of him. But after all these years left in darkness, corruption must have taken hold. || [context] NodeContext: Concerned/Urgent. The curse will not be lifted unless a spirit of the land is fully restored
Player: Tell me how I can help.
Halsin: It's both simple and not - we need to find Thaniel's missing half, and make him whole again. || [context] NodeContext: Concerned/Urgent. The curse will not be lifted unless a spirit of the land is fully restored
Halsin: Only, the missing half may not come willingly. The curse will have sunk its tendrils deep, twisting Thaniel's essence into something... else. || [context] NodeContext: Some foreboding. The curse will not be lifted unless a spirit of the land is fully restored
Player: I'll see what I can do, but no promises.

======== Scenario: moo_walltentacle ========
Session Sequence: AD_TentacleShaft -> Tentacle -> DaisyAD_FeignSuprise
----- Session: AD_TentacleShaft -----
Synopsis: The player passed a perception check to recognise tendrils of organic matter drooping through a wall. Exploring the rafters above this spot leads to the tentacle scene.

Player: Something slimy seems to be dripping from the rafters above.

----- Session: Tentacle -----
Synopsis: Upon interacting with the tentacle living inside the tower's wall, player is faced with several options to choose from. - Take a sample (can be used in Mig mini quest)- Poke to see how it reacts- Examine it to learn more about it- Tear it down with brute forceDamage being done onto the tentacle will trigger a reaction from the Absolute

Player: Determine what it is.
: True
Narrator: *You can't quite catch a glimpse, but you recognise this feeling - the same alien presence you felt on the nautiloid.*
Player: Leave.

======== Scenario: scl_mastiffpoachers ========
Session Sequence: TrueSoul_Dead
----- Session: TrueSoul_Dead -----
Synopsis: SwD dialog for dead True Soul that died of hunger/thirst while hiding from Shadow Mastiffs in the island of light. They used Continual Flame spell to make torches around them ever-burning, which allowed them to hide there indefinitely (until they died). The kicker - description of the spell says that each casting uses Ruby Dust worth 50gp, so, presumably, that's one rich True Soul.

Narrator: *The corpse regards you lifelessly.*
Player: Who were you in life?
True Soul Korliss: True Soul of the Absolute... Korliss by name...

======== Scenario: twn_finale ========
Session Sequence: LeavingAct -> PAD_ArmyLeft
----- Session: LeavingAct -----
Synopsis: Scene of players leaving SCL to travel to Intermezzo. This scene triggers when the party leave Moonrise Tower after defeating Ketheric. There are two variants. One where the curse has been lifted, one where the curse hasn't been lifted.If the curse has been lifted, Halsin and/or Art Cullagh will be present at Moonrise if alive, and will tell players that the quest has succeeded, and that when they leave Moonrise, they'll see the restults. They tell you to wrap up your business here first. This happens in the dialogues for those characters, not here.If the curse hasn't been lifted, players see a vista of the shadow-cursed lands on leaving Moonrise, and move on toward the Risen Road.

Narrator: *The curse has been lifted, the lands cleansed of the shadows. Ketheric's reign of living death is over.* || [context] CinematicNodeContext: Players leave SCL by the Risen Road. They look back to see beams of light breaking through the clouds.-The curse has been lifted. The clouds above part, and a powerful beam of moonlight shines through and illuminates the town centre where the statue of Ketheric stood. It is now shattered.
Narrator: *Your courage has been tested, and in this, at least, you have triumphed.* || [context] CinematicNodeContext: Cut to close up of the shattered statue. An enormous silver tree bursts through the ground where the statue once stood, silver leaves/fruits sprouting, and the light from above intensifies as the shadows disperse.
[desc] CinematicNodeContext: Cut back to party, with Halsin in shot, looking across the rejuvenating region. Halsin takes front and centre, looking back across the 'healed'vista, overjoyed, and then the party turn and continue their journey || [context] CinematicNodeContext: Cut back to party, with Halsin in shot, looking across the rejuvenating region. Halsin takes front and centre, looking back across the 'healed'vista, overjoyed, and then the party turn and continue their journey

----- Session: PAD_ArmyLeft -----
Synopsis: Comment on how the absolute army left. Reactivity if you saw them previously or not.

Player: The Absolute's armies are on the march - and Baldur's Gate is their target.
